Our catalog with **#20250405** (Catalog version **3.4.323** ) is available to our **Easy2Patch** customers.

This week, **65** software updates are provided in the E2P catalog. We support **478** products of **294** individual manufacturers in total. We are updating **642** products with 32/64-bit and language options.

***Note:*** *VirusTotal and Kaspersky Opentip scans are the responsibility of the manufacturer. E2P Bilisim has no responsibility or liability for the virus scanning results of the files.*

> **Kaspersky:** [GoTo: OpenTip<svg class="gb-icon ml-0.5 inline size-3 links-accent:text-tint-subtle"><title>arrow-up-right</title><defs><mask id="_R_j82539bsnqj6iv5ubsnpfivb_" style="mask-type:alpha"><image data-testid="mask-image" href="https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v7.2.0/svgs/regular/arrow-up-right.svg?v=2&token=a463935e93" width="100%" height="100%" preserveaspectratio="xMidYMid meet"></image></mask></defs><rect width="100%" height="100%" fill="currentColor" mask="url(#_R_j82539bsnqj6iv5ubsnpfivb_)"></rect></svg>](https://opentip.kaspersky.com/a31832d932b02b7ec55d9a2bf79d0080adc1675b094a328662c5b1b49ddf0ad4)
> 
> App 4.5.0-app for Windows, Mac, and Linux(released September 6th, 2022) New features - 802.1X authentication for ethernet added in setup flow and device settings - Rooms: Sign in with Google Calendar to have easier access to your meetings. - Rooms: Added the ability to join calls on Linux. Improvements - New streaming technology for Linux: WebRTC-based streaming to provide a smoother screen sharing experience and the ability to select which screen to share in multi-screen setups. This also adds support for the latest Ubuntu LTS version. - Audio on Linux is for the moment no longer supported. We will seek to add audio at a later date. Customers who wish to use audio streaming on Linux should stay on app version 4.1.1. - Added new security controls following Electron best practices, including but not limited to the prevention of untrusted resources. Bugfixes - Rooms: Fixed an issue that prevented sharing a single window to a Teams call when two overlapping windows of the same program are present, e.g. during a PowerPoint presentation - Rooms: Fixed an issue that prevented sharing content from a secondary monitor to a Teams call - Rooms: Cancelling a request to join a call in the Airtame application should now properly return the Airtame Hub to an idle state.

> 2.25.10 \* api-change:``route53``: Added us-gov-east-1 and us-gov-west-1 as valid Latency Based Routing regions for change-resource-record-sets. \* api-change:``sagemaker``: Adds support for i3en, m7i, r7i instance types for SageMaker Hyperpod \* api-change:``bedrock-agent``: Added optional "customMetadataField" for Amazon Aurora knowledge bases, allowing single-column metadata. Also added optional "textIndexName" for MongoDB Atlas knowledge bases, enabling hybrid search support.

> ISPSoft is the latest program development tool for Delta's programmable logic controllers (PLC) that complies with the IEC 61131-3 standard to integrate multiple tasks for project management. Customers can use standard PLCopen® function blocks, as well as Delta's self-developed function blocks to easily achieve different control requirements. ISPSoft offers users an efficient and convenient development environment, and is suitable for both small and complex control systems.

> Garmin Express v7.25.0 is available for PC today. If you would like to update to the latest version, please visit “About” within the Settings of the Express application and select “Check for Updates to Express.” This version includes the following changes: Added the ability to install the basemap if it’s not currently installed on the device. Added support for displaying semantic versioning. Fixed an issue on the dashboard not displaying the bubble for number of updates available. Other minor bug fixes and improvements.

> product icon About the GoTo Opener GoTo Meeting uses a "helper" application to launch you into active sessions. This application is known as the GoTo Opener app. When you install the GoTo Meeting software, this app is automatically installed on your computer as well. It will also run each time you join or start a session in order to connect you to your GoTo service. Note: The newest version of this "helper" application is named the "GoTo Opener" app, but it previously was known under another name.

> Release v1.15.9 / 5.70.9 Release Notes Sandboxie Plus 1.15.9 delivers a robust update centered on security, stability, and compatibility—particularly for users of modern web browsers and those prioritizing privacy and sandbox integrity. Firefox now runs smoothly within sandboxed environments once again.

> Release v1.15.9 / 5.70.9 Release Notes Sandboxie Plus 1.15.9 delivers a robust update centered on security, stability, and compatibility—particularly for users of modern web browsers and those prioritizing privacy and sandbox integrity. A key highlight is the improved compatibility with Firefox 137 Nightly and later, resolving previous hooking issues that caused instability or functional limitations. Firefox now runs smoothly within sandboxed environments once again.

The new enterprise scale tiers for high volume portfolios are available to Advance customers. In addition, all Control Center users will see faster project creation, archiving and improved user interface performance in support of an enterprise-grade large project portfolio manageability experience. The expanded ability to manage portfolios at unprecedented levels of scale enables PMOs and Project Directors to execute high volume projects, processes and programs consistently and meet the growing demands of their business. You can learn more about how to set up additional Control Center intake capacity in this help article. To learn more about Control Center increased upper limits and number of active projects available by plan type please see this article. > Released March 31, 2025 version 6.3.10 New, enhanced, and changed features General features New or enhanced feature VDI Plugin Management version display Users can view the installed version of Virtual Desktop Infrastructure Plugin Management in the VDI Statistics tab. This indication helps users quickly determine if they need to install VDI Plugin Management on their virtual desktop.

> Azul Zulu 24 General AvailabilityRelease Notes What’s New OpenJDK OpenJDK 24 is a Short Term Support (STS) release that Azul supports until September 2025 as indicated on our Support Roadmap. This version brings 14 new features and 10 new or extensions of earlier incubator and preview features. Further, it contains over 2800 general fixes and performance improvements.

> Azul Zulu 24 General AvailabilityRelease Notes What’s New OpenJDK OpenJDK 24 is a Short Term Support (STS) release that Azul supports until September 2025 as indicated on our Support Roadmap. This version brings 14 new features and 10 new or extensions of earlier incubator and preview features. Further, it contains over 2800 general fixes and performance improvements.
